<br/>\n         1790\xe2\x80\x931960\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n          <a href="#cite_note-42">\n           [40]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         1900\xe2\x80\x931990\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n          <a href="#cite_note-43">\n           [41]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <br/>\n         1990\xe2\x80\x932000\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n          <a href="#cite_note-44">\n           [42]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <br/>\n         <a class="external autonumber" href="http://factfinder.census.gov/faces/tableservices/jsf/pages/productview.xhtml?pid=PEP_2015_PEPANNRES&amp;prodType=table" rel="nofollow">\n          [3]\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:USA_Norfolk_city,_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="520" height="231" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg/200px-USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg/300px-USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg/400px-USA_Norfolk_city%2C_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg.png 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:USA_Norfolk_city,_Virginia_age_pyramid.svg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Population age distribution for Norfolk\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">\n        census\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GR8_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GR8-45">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       of 2010, there were 242,803 people, 86,210 households, and 51,898 families residing in the city. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Population_density" title="Population density">\n        population density\n       </a>\n       was 4,362.8 people per square mile (1,684.4/km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ). There were 94,416 housing units at an average density of 1,757.3 per square mile (678.5/km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ). The racial makeup of the city was 47.1%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_American" title="European American">\n        European American\n       </a>\n       , 43.1%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n        African American\n       </a>\n       , 0.5%\n       <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">\n        Native American\n       </a>\n       , 3.3%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n        Asian\n       </a>\n       , 0.2%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Islander_American" title="Pacific Islander American">\n        Pacific Islander\n       </a>\n       , 2.2% from\n       <a href="/wiki/Race_and_ethnicity_in_the_United_States_Census" title="Race and ethnicity in the United States Census">\n        other races\n       </a>\n       , and 3.6% from two or more races.\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_and_Latino_Americans" title="Hispanic and Latino Americans">\n        Hispanics or Latinos\n       </a>\n       of any race were 6.6% of the population.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-Hispanic_Whites" title="Non-Hispanic Whites">\n        Non-Hispanic Whites\n       </a>\n       were 44.3% of the population in 2010,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       down from 68.5% in 1970.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There were 86,210 households out of which 30.3% had children under the age of 18 living with them, 36.9% were\n       <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">\n        married couples\n       </a>\n       living together, 18.8% had a female householder with no husband present, and 39.8% were non-families. 30.2% of all households were made up of individuals and 9.6% had someone living alone who was 65 years of age or older. The average household size was 2.45 and the average family size was 3.07.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The age distribution was 24.0% under the age of 18, 18.2% from 18 to 24, 29.9% from 25 to 44, 16.9% from 45 to 64, and 10.9% who were 65 years of age or older. The median age was 30 years. For every 100 females, there were 104.6 males. For every 100 females age 18 and over, there were 104.8 males. This large\n       <a href="/wiki/Sex_ratio" title="Sex ratio">\n        gender imbalance\n       </a>\n       is due to the military presence in the city, most notably Naval Station Norfolk.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The median income for a household in the city was $31,815, and the median income for a family was $36,891. Males had a median income of $25,848 versus $21,907 for females. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Per_capita_income" title="Per capita income">\n        per capita income\n       </a>\n       for the city was $17,372. About 15.5% of families and 19.4% of the population were below the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Poverty_line" title="Poverty line">\n        poverty line\n       </a>\n       , including 27.9% of those under age 18 and 13.2% of those ages 65 or over.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       For the year of 2007, Norfolk had a total crime index of 514.7 per 100,000 residents. This was above the national average of 320.9 that year. For 2007, the city experienced 48 homicides, for a murder rate of 21.1 per 100,000 residents. Total crime had decreased when compared to the year 2000, which the city had a total crime index of 546.3. The highest murder rate Norfolk has experienced for the 21st century was in 2005 when its rate was 24.5 per 100,000 residents. For the year 2007 per 100,000, Norfolk experienced 21.1 murders, 42.6 rapes, 399.3 robberies, 381.3 assaults, 743.3 burglaries, and 450.6 automobile thefts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to the Congressional Quarterly Press \'2008 City Crime Rankings: Crime in Metropolitan America, Norfolk, Virginia, ranked as the 87th most dangerous city larger than 75,000 inhabitants.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">\n        Economy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Economy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Norfolk,_Virginia" title="Economy of Norfolk, Virginia">\n        Economy of Norfolk, Virginia\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1464" data-file-width="1780" height="181" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg/220px-1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg/330px-1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg/440px-1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1888_Great_Atlantic_and_Pacific_Tea_Co_Advert_for_Norfolk.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         1888 advertisement for the Market Square\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/A%26P" title="A&amp;P">\n          A&amp;P\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Since Norfolk serves as the commercial and cultural center for the unusual geographical region of Hampton Roads (and in its political structure of independent cities), it can be difficult to separate the economic characteristics of Norfolk from that of the region as a whole.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The waterways which almost completely surround the Hampton Roads region play an important part in the local economy. As a strategic location at the mouth of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       , its protected deep-water channels serve as a major trade artery for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Import" title="Import">\n        import\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Export" title="Export">\n        export\n       </a>\n       of goods from across the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_States" title="Mid-Atlantic States">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">\n        Mid-West\n       </a>\n       , and internationally.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Global_Security_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Global_Security-50">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In addition to commercial activities, Hampton Roads is a major military center, particularly for the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">\n        United States Navy\n       </a>\n       , and Norfolk serves as the home for\n       <a href="/wiki/Naval_Station_Norfolk" title="Naval Station Norfolk">\n        Naval Station Norfolk\n       </a>\n       , the world\'s largest naval installation. Located on\n       <a href="/wiki/Sewell%27s_Point" title="Sewell\'s Point">\n        Sewell\'s Point Peninsula\n       </a>\n       , in the northwest corner of the city, the station is the headquarters of the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Fleet_Forces_Command" title="United States Fleet Forces Command">\n        United States Fleet Forces Command\n       </a>\n       (formerly known as the Atlantic Fleet), which compromises over 62,000 active duty personnel, 75 ships, and 132 aircraft. The base also serves as the headquarters to\n       <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">\n        NATO\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Allied_Command_Transformation" title="Allied Command Transformation">\n        Allied Command Transformation\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The region also plays an important role in defense contracting, with particular emphasis in the shipbuilding and ship repair businesses for the city of Norfolk. Major private shipyards located in Norfolk or the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads" title="Hampton Roads">\n        Hampton Roads\n       </a>\n       area include:\n       <a href="/wiki/Huntington_Ingalls_Industries" title="Huntington Ingalls Industries">\n        Huntington Ingalls Industries\n       </a>\n       (formerly Northrop Grumman Newport News) in Newport News,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Ship_Repair" title="BAE Systems Ship Repair">\n        BAE Systems Norfolk Ship Repair\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/General_Dynamics" title="General Dynamics">\n        General Dynamics\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Steel_and_Shipbuilding_Company" title="National Steel and Shipbuilding Company">\n        NASSCO\n       </a>\n       Norfolk, and Colonna\'s Shipyard Inc., while the US Navy\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Naval_Shipyard" title="Norfolk Naval Shipyard">\n        Norfolk Naval Shipyard\n       </a>\n       is just across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Downtown_Tunnel" title="Downtown Tunnel">\n        Downtown Tunnel\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_Virginia" title="Portsmouth, Virginia">\n        Portsmouth\n       </a>\n       . Most contracts fulfilled by these shipyards are issued by the Navy, though some private commercial repair also takes place. Over 35% of Gross Regional Product (which includes the entire Norfolk-Newport News-Virginia Beach MSA), is attributable to defense spending, and that 75% of all regional growth since 2001 is attributable to increases in defense spending.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_Statistics_52-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_Statistics-52">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Norfolk,_VA.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2099" data-file-width="2620" height="176" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg/220px-Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg/330px-Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg/440px-Norfolk%2C_VA.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Norfolk,_VA.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A view of Norfolk from Portsmouth\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       After the military, the second largest and most important industry for Hampton Roads and Norfolk based on economic impact are the region\'s cargo ports. Headquartered in Norfolk, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Port_Authority" title="Virginia Port Authority">\n        Virginia Port Authority\n       </a>\n       (VPA) is a\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Commonwealth of Virginia\n       </a>\n       owned-entity that, in turn, owns and operates three major port facilities in Hampton Roads for break-bulk and container type cargo. In Norfolk,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norfolk_International_Terminals" title="Norfolk International Terminals">\n        Norfolk International Terminals\n       </a>\n       (NIT) represents one of those three facilities and is home to the world\'s largest and fastest container cranes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIT_Facilities_53-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NIT_Facilities-53">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Together, the three terminals of the VPA handled a total of over 2 million\n       <a href="/wiki/Containerization" title="Containerization">\n        TEUs\n       </a>\n       and 475,000 tons of breakbulk cargo in 2006, making it the second busiest port on the east coast of North America by total cargo volume after the Port of New York and New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_Ports_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_Ports-54">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In addition to NIT, Norfolk is home to Lambert\'s Point Docks, the largest coal trans-shipment point in the Northern Hemisphere, with an annual throughput of approximately 48,000,000 tons.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lamberts_Point_55-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Lamberts_Point-55">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Bituminous_coal" title="Bituminous coal">\n        Bituminous coal\n       </a>\n       is primarily sourced from the Appalachian mountains in western Virginia,\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Kentucky" title="Kentucky">\n        Kentucky\n       </a>\n       . The coal is loaded onto trains and sent to the port where it is unloaded onto large breakbulk cargo ships and destined for New England, Europe, and Asia.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Between 1925 and 2007,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor_Company" title="Ford Motor Company">\n        Ford Motor Company\n       </a>\n       operated\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Assembly" title="Norfolk Assembly">\n        Norfolk Assembly\n       </a>\n       , a manufacturing plant located on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_River_(Virginia)" title="Elizabeth River (Virginia)">\n        Elizabeth River\n       </a>\n       that had produced the Model-T, sedans and station wagons before building F-150 pick-up trucks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vp1_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-vp1-56">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Before it closed, the plant employed more than 2,600 people at the 2,800,000-square-foot (260,000\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) facility.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vp1_56-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-vp1-56">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vp1_56-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-vp1-56">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Trader_Square,_Norfolk.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2272" data-file-width="1704" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG/220px-Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG/330px-Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG/440px-Trader_Square%2C_Norfolk.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Trader_Square,_Norfolk.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Dominion Square, headquarters of\n         <a href="/wiki/Dominion_Enterprises" title="Dominion Enterprises">\n          Dominion Enterprises\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Most major shipping lines have a permanent presence in the region with some combination of sales, distribution, and/or logistical offices, many of which are located in Norfolk. In addition, many of the largest international shipping companies have chosen Norfolk as their North American headquarters. These companies are either located at the Norfolk World Trade Center building or have constructed buildings in the Lake Wright Executive Center\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Office_park" title="Office park">\n        office park\n       </a>\n       . The French firm\n       <a href="/wiki/CMA_CGM" title="CMA CGM">\n        CMA CGM\n       </a>\n       , the Israeli firm\n       <a href="/wiki/Zim_Integrated_Shipping_Services" title="Zim Integrated Shipping Services">\n        Zim Integrated Shipping Services\n       </a>\n       , and Maersk Line Limited, a subsidiary of the world\'s largest shipping line,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/A._P._Moller-Maersk_Group" title="A. P. Moller-Maersk Group">\n        A. P. Moller-Maersk Group\n       </a>\n       , have their North American headquarters in Norfolk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CMA_CGM_Picks_Norfolk_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CMA_CGM_Picks_Norfolk-57">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Zin_American_Israeli_Shipping_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Zin_American_Israeli_Shipping-58">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maersk_Line_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Maersk_Line-59">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Major companies headquartered in Norfolk include\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norfolk_Southern" title="Norfolk Southern">\n        Norfolk Southern\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Southern_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Southern-60">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Landmark_Media_Enterprises" title="Landmark Media Enterprises">\n        Landmark Communications\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Landmark_Communications_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Landmark_Communications-61">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominion_Enterprises" title="Dominion Enterprises">\n        Dominion Enterprises\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominion_Enterprises_62-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominion_Enterprises-62">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       FHC Health Systems (parent company of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ValueOptions" title="ValueOptions">\n        ValueOptions\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FHC_Health_Systems_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FHC_Health_Systems-63">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Portfolio Recovery Associates,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Portfolio_Recovery_Associates_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Portfolio_Recovery_Associates-64">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and BlackHawk Products Group.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BlackHawk_Products_Group_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-BlackHawk_Products_Group-65">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wisconsin_museum.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Wisconsin_museum.JPG/220px-Wisconsin_museum.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Wisconsin_museum.JPG/330px-Wisconsin_museum.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Wisconsin_museum.JPG/440px-Wisconsin_museum.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wisconsin_museum.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Nauticus and\n         <a href="/wiki/USS_Wisconsin_(BB-64)" title="USS Wisconsin (BB-64)">\n          USS\n          <i>\n           Wisconsin\n          </i>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Though\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach" title="Virginia Beach">\n        Virginia Beach\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Williamsburg,_Virginia" title="Williamsburg, Virginia">\n        Williamsburg\n       </a>\n       have traditionally been the centers of tourism for the region, the rebirth of downtown Norfolk and the construction of a cruise ship pier at the foot of\n       <a href="/wiki/Nauticus" title="Nauticus">\n        Nauticus\n       </a>\n       in downtown has driven tourism to become an increasingly important part of the city\'s economy. The number of cruise ship passengers who visited Norfolk increased from 50,000 in 2003, to 107,000 in 2004 and 2005. Also in April 2007, the city completed construction on a $36 million state-of-the-art cruise ship terminal alongside the pier.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Half_Moone_Terminal_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Half_Moone_Terminal-66">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Partly due to this construction, passenger counts dropped to 70,000 in 2006, but is expected to rebound to 90,000 in 2007, and higher in later years. Unlike most cruise ship terminals which are located in industrial areas, the downtown location of Norfolk\'s terminal has received favorable reviews from both tourists and the cruise lines who enjoy its proximity to the city\'s hotels, restaurants, shopping, and cultural amenities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cruise_Norfolk_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Cruise_Norfolk-67">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hampton Roads is home to four Fortune 500 companies. Representing the food industry, transportation, retail and shipbuilding, these four companies are located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Smithfield,_Virginia" title="Smithfield, Virginia">\n        Smithfield\n       </a>\n       , Norfolk,\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake,_Virginia" title="Chesapeake, Virginia">\n        Chesapeake\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Newport_News" title="Newport News">\n        Newport News\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div>\n       <table class="multicol" role="presentation" style=\'"border-collapse:\'>\n     380\n        <a href="/wiki/Huntington_Ingalls_Industries" title="Huntington Ingalls Industries">\n         Huntington Ingalls Industries\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n Kennedy (CV-67)">\n          USS\n          <i>\n           John F. Kennedy\n          </i>\n          (CV-67)\n         </a>\n         arriving at Naval Station Norfolk\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       According to a report published by the Virginia Employment Commission,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       below are the top employers title="PRA Group">\n          Portfolio Recovery Associates\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Arts_and_culture">\n        Arts and culture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Arts and culture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Culture_in_Norfolk,_Virginia" title="Culture in Norfolk, Virginia">\n        Culture in Norfolk, Virginia\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MacArthurStatue.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="590" data-file-width="400" height="325" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/MacArthurStatue.jpg/220px-MacArthurStatue.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/MacArthurStatue.jpg/330px-MacArthurStatue.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/7a/MacArthurStatue.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MacArthurStatue.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">\n          Douglas MacArthur\n         </a>\n         Statue\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is the cultural heart of the Hampton Roads region. In addition to its museums, Norfolk is the principal home for several major performing arts companies. Norfolk also plays host to numerous yearly festivals and parades, mostly at Town Point Park in downtown.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_Museum_of_Art" title="Chrysler Museum of Art">\n        Chrysler Museum of Art\n       </a>\n       , located in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ghent_district" title="Ghent district">\n        Ghent district\n       </a>\n       , is the region\'s foremost art museum and is considered by\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">\n         The New York Times\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       to be the finest in the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Travel_Guide_70-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Travel_Guide-70">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Of particular note is the extensive glass collection, the Glass Studio,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chrysler_Museum_Glass_Studio_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chrysler_Museum_Glass_Studio-71">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the Moses Myers House, and American\n       <a href="/wiki/Neoclassicism" title="Neoclassicism">\n        neoclassical\n       </a>\n       marble sculptures. The museum\'s main building is undergoing expansion and renovation and is expected to reopen in April 2014. During the renovation, the Glass Studio and the Moses Myers House will remain open and art will be displayed at venues throughout the community.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chrysler_Museum_Renovation_72-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chrysler_Museum_Renovation-72">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chrysler_Museum_Road_Show_73-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chrysler_Museum_Road_Show-73">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Nauticus" title="Nauticus">\n        Nauticus\n       </a>\n       , the National Maritime Center, opened on the downtown waterfront in 1994. It features hands-on exhibits, interactive theaters,\n       <a href="/wiki/Aquarium" title="Aquarium">\n        aquaria\n       </a>\n       , digital high-definition films and an extensive variety of educational programs. Since 2000, Nauticus has been home to the battleship\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Wisconsin_(BB-64)" title="USS Wisconsin (BB-64)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Wisconsin\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , the last battleship to be built in the United States. It served briefly in\n       <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">\n        World War II\n       </a>\n       and later in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Korean_War" title="Korean War">\n        Korean\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_War" title="Gulf War">\n        Gulf Wars\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nauticus_74-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Nauticus-74">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_City_Hall" title="Norfolk City Hall">\n        MacArthur Memorial\n       </a>\n       , located in the nineteenth century Norfolk courthouse and city hall in downtown, contains the tombs of the late\n       <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">\n        General\n       </a>\n       and his wife, a museum and a vast research library, personal belongings (including his famous corncob pipe) and a short film that chronicles the life of the famous\n       <a href="/wiki/General_of_the_Army_(United_States)" title="General of the Army (United States)">\n        General of the Army\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MacArthur_Memorial_75-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MacArthur_Memorial-75">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/People_for_the_Ethical_Treatment_of_Animals" title="People for the Ethical Treatment of Animals">\n        People for the Ethical Treatment of Animals\n       </a>\n       (PETA), the world\'s largest animal rights organization, is based in Norfolk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Hermitage Foundation Museum, located in an early 20th-century\n       <a href="/wiki/Tudor_Revival_architecture" title="Tudor Revival architecture">\n        Tudor-style\n       </a>\n       home on a 12-acre (49,000\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) estate fronting the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lafayette_River" title="Lafayette River">\n        Lafayette River\n       </a>\n       , features an eclectic collection of Asian and Western art, including Chinese bronze and ceramics, Persian rugs, and ivory carvings.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Norfolk has a variety of performing groups with regular seasons.\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harrison_operahouse.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="306" data-file-width="460" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Harrison_operahouse.jpg/220px-Harrison_operahouse.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Harrison_operahouse.jpg/330px-Harrison_operahouse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Harrison_operahouse.jpg/440px-Harrison_operahouse.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harrison_operahouse.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Harrison Opera House\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nauticus,_Norfolk.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="2272" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG/220px-Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG/330px-Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG/440px-Nauticus%2C_Norfolk.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nauticus,_Norfolk.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Nauticus" title="Nauticus">\n          Nauticus\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Opera" title="Virginia Opera">\n        Virginia Opera\n       </a>\n       was founded in Norfolk in 1974. Its artistic director since its inception has been Peter Mark,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       who conducted his 100th opera production for the VOA in 2008. Though performances are staged statewide, the company\'s principal venue is the\n       <a href="/wiki/Harrison_Opera_House" title="Harrison Opera House">\n        Harrison Opera House\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ghent_district" title="Ghent district">\n        Ghent district\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Virginia_Opera_79-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Virginia_Opera-79">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Virginia Stage Company, founded in 1968, is one of the country\'s leading regional theaters and produces a full season of plays in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Wells_Theatre" title="Wells Theatre">\n        Wells Theatre\n       </a>\n       downtown. The company shares facilities with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor%27s_School_for_the_Arts" title="Governor\'s School for the Arts">\n        Governor\'s School for the Arts\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Virginia_Stage_Company_80-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Virginia_Stage_Company-80">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Symphony_Orchestra" title="Virginia Symphony Orchestra">\n        Virginia Symphony Orchestra\n       </a>\n       , founded in 1920 and directed by\n       <a href="/wiki/JoAnn_Falletta" title="JoAnn Falletta">\n        JoAnn Falletta\n       </a>\n       , has been a regular staple on the regional fine arts scene. Most Norfolk performances take place at\n       <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_Hall" title="Chrysler Hall">\n        Chrysler Hall\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Scope" title="Norfolk Scope">\n        Scope\n       </a>\n       complex downtown. The orchestra also provides musicians for many other performing arts organizations in the area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Virginia_Symphony_81-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Virginia_Symphony-81">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Large-scale concerts are held at either the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Scope" title="Norfolk Scope">\n        Norfolk Scope\n       </a>\n       arena or the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ted_Constant_Convocation_Center" title="Ted Constant Convocation Center">\n        Ted Constant Convocation Center\n       </a>\n       at\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_University" title="Old Dominion University">\n        ODU\n       </a>\n       , while\n       <a href="/wiki/Norva_Theatre" title="Norva Theatre">\n        The Norva\n       </a>\n       provides a more intimate atmosphere for smaller groups. Other Norfolk cultural venues include the\n       <a href="/wiki/Attucks_Theatre" title="Attucks Theatre">\n        Attucks Theatre\n       </a>\n       , the Jeanne and George Roper Performing Arts Canter (formerly the Loew\'s State Theater) and the Naro Expanded Cinema.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The revitalization of downtown Norfolk has helped to improve the Hampton Roads cultural scene. In particular, a large number of clubs, representing a wide range of music interests and sophistication now line the lower Granby Street area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nightlife_and_Entertainment_in_Downtown_Norfolk_82-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Nightlife_and_Entertainment_in_Downtown_Norfolk-82">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk celebrates the rich ethnic diversity of its population with sights, sounds, attractions and special events that pay tribute to the city\'s long multicultural heritage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n        <a href="#cite_note-83">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Sports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harbor_park.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="861" data-file-width="1200" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Harbor_park.jpg/220px-Harbor_park.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Harbor_park.jpg/330px-Harbor_park.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Harbor_park.jpg/440px-Harbor_park.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harbor_park.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Harbor_Park" title="Harbor Park">\n          Harbor Park\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Norfolk,_Virginia" title="Sports in Norfolk, Virginia">\n        Sports in Norfolk, Virginia\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk serves as home to the two highest level professional franchises in the state of Virginia \xe2\x80\x94 the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Tides" title="Norfolk Tides">\n        Norfolk Tides\n       </a>\n       plays Triple-A baseball in the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_League" title="International League">\n        International League\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Admirals_(ECHL)" title="Norfolk Admirals (ECHL)">\n        Norfolk Admirals\n       </a>\n       play ice hockey in the\n       <a href="/wiki/ECHL" title="ECHL">\n        ECHL\n       </a>\n       . Norfolk has two universities with Division I sports teams \xe2\x80\x94 the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_Monarchs" title="Old Dominion Monarchs">\n        Old Dominion Monarchs\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_State_University" title="Norfolk State University">\n        Norfolk State University\n       </a>\n       Spartans, which provide many sports including football, basketball, and baseball.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Admirals_84-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Admirals-84">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tides_85-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Tides-85">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Monarchs_86-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Monarchs-86">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Spartans_87-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Spartans-87">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Marlins_88-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Marlins-88">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       From 1970 to 76, Norfolk served as the home court (along with\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton,_Virginia" title="Hampton, Virginia">\n        Hampton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">\n        Richmond\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Roanoke,_Virginia" title="Roanoke, Virginia">\n        Roanoke\n       </a>\n       ) for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Squires" title="Virginia Squires">\n        Virginia Squires\n       </a>\n       regional professional basketball franchise of the now-defunct\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Basketball_Association" title="American Basketball Association">\n        American Basketball Association\n       </a>\n       (ABA). From 1970 to 71, the Squires played their Norfolk home games at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_University_Fieldhouse" title="Old Dominion University Fieldhouse">\n        Old Dominion University Fieldhouse\n       </a>\n       . In November 1971, the Virginia Squires played their Norfolk home games at the new\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Scope" title="Norfolk Scope">\n        Norfolk Scope\n       </a>\n       arena, until the team and the ABA league folded in May 1976.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 1971, Norfolk built an entertainment and sports complex, featuring\n       <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_Hall" title="Chrysler Hall">\n        Chrysler Hall\n       </a>\n       and the 13,800-seat\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Scope" title="Norfolk Scope">\n        Norfolk Scope\n       </a>\n       indoor arena, located in the northern section of downtown. Norfolk Scope has served as a venue for major events including the American Basketball Association\'s All-Star Game in 1974,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the first and second\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NCAA_Women%27s_Division_I_Basketball_Championship" title="NCAA Women\'s Division I Basketball Championship">\n        NCAA Women\'s Division I Basketball Championships\n       </a>\n       (also known as the\n       <i>\n        Women\'s Final Four\n       </i>\n       ) in 1982 and 1983.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1983tourney_92-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1983tourney-92">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is also home to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Blues" title="Norfolk Blues">\n        Norfolk Blues\n       </a>\n       Rugby Football Club.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Parks_and_recreation">\n        Parks and recreation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Parks and recreation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3008" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg/220px-NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg/330px-NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg/440px-NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NorfolkBotanicalGardenCanal.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Canal at the Norfolk Botanical Garden\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Town_Point_Park" title="Town Point Park">\n        Town Point Park\n       </a>\n       in downtown plays host to a wide variety of annual events from early spring through late fall. Harborfest, the region\'s largest annual festival, celebrated its thirtieth anniversary in 2006. It is held during the first weekend of June and celebrates the region\'s proximity and attachment to the water. The Parade of Sail (numerous tall sailing ships from around the world form in line and sail past downtown before docking at the marina), music concerts, regional food, and a large fireworks display highlight this three-day festival.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festevents_93-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Festevents-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Bayou Boogaloo and Cajun Food Festival, a celebration of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cajun" title="Cajun">\n        Cajun\n       </a>\n       people and culture, had small beginnings. This three-day festival during the third week of June has become one of the largest in the region and, in addition to serving up\n       <a href="/wiki/Cajun_cuisine" title="Cajun cuisine">\n        Cajun cuisine\n       </a>\n       , also features Cajun music.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festevents_93-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Festevents-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Norfolk\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Independence_Day_(United_States)" title="Independence Day (United States)">\n        Fourth of July\n       </a>\n       celebration of American independence contains a spectacular fireworks display and a special Navy reenlistment ceremony.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festevents_93-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Festevents-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Norfolk Jazz Festival, though smaller by comparison to some of the big city jazz festivals, still manages to attract the country\'s top jazz performers. It is held in August.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festevents_93-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Festevents-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Town Point Virginia Wine Festival has become a showcase for Virginia-produced wines and has enjoyed increasing success over the years. Virginia\'s burgeoning wine industry has become noted both within the United States and on an international level. The festival has grown with the industry. Wines can be sampled and then purchased by the bottle and/or case directly from the winery kiosks. This event takes place during the third weekend of October. There is also a Spring Wine Festival held during the second weekend of May.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festevents_93-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Festevents-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nearby are the\n       <a href="/wiki/Museum_ship" title="Museum ship">\n        museum ship\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Wisconsin_(BB-64)" title="USS Wisconsin (BB-64)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Wisconsin\n        </i>\n        (BB-64)\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin_Square" title="Wisconsin Square">\n        Wisconsin Square\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Patrick%27s_Day" title="St. Patrick\'s Day">\n        St. Patrick\'s Day\n       </a>\n       annual parade in the city\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocean_View,_Virginia" title="Ocean View, Virginia">\n        Ocean View\n       </a>\n       neighborhood, celebrates Ocean View\'s rich Irish heritage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_St._Patrick.27s_Day_Parade_94-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_St._Patrick.27s_Day_Parade-94">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="493" data-file-width="800" height="136" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg/220px-Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg/330px-Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg/440px-Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Norfolk_Zoo_Entrance.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Virginia Zoo\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk has a variety of parks\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and open spaces in its city parks system. The city maintains three beaches on its north shore in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocean_View,_Virginia" title="Ocean View, Virginia">\n        Ocean View\n       </a>\n       area. Five additional parks contain picnic facilities and playgrounds for children. The city also has some community pools open to city residents.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Parks_96-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Parks-96">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Botanical_Garden" title="Norfolk Botanical Garden">\n        Norfolk Botanical Garden\n       </a>\n       , opened in 1939, is a 155-acre (0.6\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       )\n       <a href="/wiki/Botanical_garden" title="Botanical garden">\n        botanical garden\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Arboretum" title="Arboretum">\n        arboretum\n       </a>\n       located near the Norfolk International Airport. It is open year-round.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Botanical_Gardens_97-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Botanical_Gardens-97">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Zoo" title="Virginia Zoo">\n        Virginia Zoological Park\n       </a>\n       , opened in 1900, is a 65-acre (260,000\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       )\n       <a href="/wiki/Zoo" title="Zoo">\n        zoo\n       </a>\n       with hundreds of animals on display, including the critically endangered\n       <a href="/wiki/Siberian_tiger" title="Siberian tiger">\n        Siberian tiger\n       </a>\n       and threatened\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_rhino" title="White rhino">\n        white rhino\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Virginia_Zoo_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Virginia_Zoo-98">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The city is also known for its "\n       <span id="Mermaids_on_Parade">\n        Mermaids on Parade\n       </span>\n       ," a public art program launched in 2002 to place mermaid statues all over the city. Tourists can take a walking tour of downtown and locate 17 mermaids while others can be found further afield.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mermaids_on_Parade_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mermaids_on_Parade-99">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government">\n        Government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table align="center" border="2" cellpadding="4" cellspacing="0" style="float:right; background:honeyDew;">\n         11.7%\n         <i>\n          494\n         </i>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is an\n       <a href="/wiki/Independent_city#Virginia" title="Independent city">\n        independent city\n       </a>\n       with services that both counties and cities in Virginia provide, such as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Sheriff" title="Sheriff">\n        sheriff\n       </a>\n       , social services, and a court system. Norfolk operates under a council-manager form of government.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk city government consists of a\n       <a href="/wiki/City_council" title="City council">\n        city council\n       </a>\n       with representatives from seven districts serving in a\n       <a href="/wiki/Legislature" title="Legislature">\n        legislative\n       </a>\n       and oversight capacity, as well as a popularly elected, at-large\n       <a href="/wiki/Mayor" title="Mayor">\n        mayor\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/City_manager" title="City manager">\n        city manager\n       </a>\n       serves as head of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Executive_(government)" title="Executive (government)">\n        executive branch\n       </a>\n       and supervises all city departments and executing policies adopted by the Council. Citizens in each of the five wards elect one council representative each to serve a four-year term. There are two additional council members elected from two citywide "Superwards." The city council meets at City Hall weekly\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_City_Council_101-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_City_Council-101">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and, as of May 2016, consists of: Mayor Kenneth Cooper Alexander; Mamie Johnson, Ward 3; Angelia Williams, Superward 7; Paul R. Riddick, Ward 4; Vice Mayor Dr. Theresa W. Whibley, Ward 2; Martin Thomas, Ward 1; Andria McClellan, Superward 6; Thomas R. Smigiel, Jr., Ward 5.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_City_Council_101-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_City_Council-101">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="border:none;">\n       <div class="NavHead" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;background:#F8F8FF;width:60%">\n        List of mayors of Norfolk, Virginia\n       </div>\n       <div class="NavContent" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;">\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          Samuel Boush, 1736 (died in office)\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n           <a href="#cite_note-102">\n            [100]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          George Newton, 1736 etc.\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          John Hutchings, 1737 etc.\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tyler1915_103-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-Tyler1915-103">\n Banks, 1888-1890\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Brant1893_107-1">\n           <a href="#cite_note-Brant1893-107">\n            [105]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          E.M. Gurkin\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          Joseph D. Wood, 1940-1944\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          James W. Reed\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          R.D. Hill">\n           Irvine B.
