Thomas\n          </a>\n          , 1976-1984\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          Joseph A. Leafe\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Mason_Andrews" title="Mason Andrews">\n           Mason Andrews\n          </a>\n          , 1992-1994\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n           <a href="#cite_note-111">\n            [109]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Paul_D._Fraim" title="Paul D. Fraim">\n           Paul D. Fraim\n          </a>\n          , 1994-2016\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n           <a href="#cite_note-112">\n            [110]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Kenneth_Cooper_Alexander" title="Kenneth Cooper Alexander">\n           Kenneth Cooper Alexander\n          </a>\n          , 2016-\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The City government has an infrastructure to create close working relationships with its citizens. Norfolk\'s city government provides services for neighborhoods, including service centers and civic leagues that interact directly with members of City Council. Such services include preserving area histories, home rehabilitation centers, outreach programs, and a university that trains citizens in neighborhood clean-up, event planning, neighborhood leadership, and financial planning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Neighborhoods_113-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Neighborhoods-113">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Norfolk\'s police department also provides support for neighborhood watch programs including a citizens\' training academy, security design, a police athletic program for youth, and business watch programs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Neighborhood_Police_114-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Neighborhood_Police-114">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk also has a federal courthouse for the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Eastern_District_of_Virginia" title="United States District Court for the Eastern District of Virginia">\n        United States District Court for the Eastern District of Virginia\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Walter_E._Hoffman_U.S._Courthouse" title="Walter E. Hoffman U.S. Courthouse">\n        Walter E. Hoffman U.S. Courthouse\n       </a>\n       in Norfolk has four judges, four magistrate judges, and two bankruptcy judges.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally, Norfolk has its own General District and Circuit Courts which convene downtown.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia%27s_2nd_congressional_district" title="Virginia\'s 2nd congressional district">\n        Virginia\'s 2nd congressional district\n       </a>\n       , served by U.S. Representative\n       <a href="/wiki/Scott_Taylor_(politician)" title="Scott Taylor (politician)">\n        Scott Taylor\n       </a>\n       (Republican) and in\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia%27s_3rd_congressional_district" title="Virginia\'s 3rd congressional district">\n        Virginia\'s 3rd congressional district\n       </a>\n       , served by U.S. Representative\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robert_C._Scott" title="Robert C. Scott">\n        Robert C. Scott\n       </a>\n       (Democrat).\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">\n        Education\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Education">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Norfolk,_Virginia" title="Education in Norfolk, Virginia">\n        Education in Norfolk, Virginia\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk City Public Schools, the public school system, comprises five high schools, eight middle schools, 34 elementary schools, and nine special-purpose/preschools. In 2005, Norfolk Public Schools won the $1 million Broad Prize for Urban Education award for having demonstrated, "the greatest overall performance and improvement in student achievement while reducing achievement gaps for poor and minority students".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Broad_Prize_for_Urban_Education_Award_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Broad_Prize_for_Urban_Education_Award-117">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city had previously been nominated in 2003 and 2004. There are also a number of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Private_schools" title="Private schools">\n        private schools\n       </a>\n       located in the city, the oldest of which,\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Academy" title="Norfolk Academy">\n        Norfolk Academy\n       </a>\n       , was founded in 1728. Religious schools located in the city include St. Pius X Catholic School, Alliance Christian School, Christ the King School,\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Christian_Schools" title="Norfolk Christian Schools">\n        Norfolk Christian Schools\n       </a>\n       and Trinity Lutheran School.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Private_Schools_118-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Private_Schools-118">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city also hosts the\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor%27s_School_for_the_Arts" title="Governor\'s School for the Arts">\n        Governor\'s School for the Arts\n       </a>\n       which holds performances and classes at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Wells_Theatre" title="Wells Theatre">\n        Wells Theatre\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jones-200wide.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="150" data-file-width="200" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/14/Jones-200wide.jpg" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         The Jones Institute for Reproductive Medicine at Eastern Virginia Medical School\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is home to three public universities and one private. It also hosts a\n       <a href="/wiki/Community_college" title="Community college">\n        community college\n       </a>\n       campus in downtown.\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_University" title="Old Dominion University">\n        Old Dominion University\n       </a>\n       , founded as the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/College_of_William_and_Mary" title="College of William and Mary">\n        Norfolk Division of the College of William and Mary\n       </a>\n       in 1930, became an independent institution in 1962 and now offers degrees in 68 undergraduate and 95 (60 masters/35 doctoral) graduate degree programs.\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Virginia_Medical_School" title="Eastern Virginia Medical School">\n        Eastern Virginia Medical School\n       </a>\n       , founded as a community medical school by the surrounding jurisdictions in 1973, is noted for its research into reproductive medicine\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-About_Jones_Institute_119-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-About_Jones_Institute-119">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and is located in the region\'s major medical complex in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ghent_district" title="Ghent district">\n        Ghent district\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_State_University" title="Norfolk State University">\n        Norfolk State University\n       </a>\n       founded in 1935 is the largest HBCU in Virginia. Norfolk State offers degrees in a wide variety of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liberal_arts" title="Liberal arts">\n        liberal arts\n       </a>\n       , Social Work, Nursing, and Engineering.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AboutNSU_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AboutNSU-120">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Wesleyan_College" title="Virginia Wesleyan College">\n        Virginia Wesleyan College\n       </a>\n       is a small private\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liberal_arts" title="Liberal arts">\n        liberal arts\n       </a>\n       college and shares its eastern border with the neighboring city of Virginia Beach.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-About_VWU_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-About_VWU-121">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Tidewater_Community_College" title="Tidewater Community College">\n        Tidewater Community College\n       </a>\n       offers two-year degrees and specialized training programs and is located in downtown. Additionally, several for-profit schools operate in the city.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Norfolk_Public_Library">\n        Norfolk Public Library\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Norfolk Public Library">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk Public Library, Virginia\'s first public library, consists of one main library, one anchor library, ten branch libraries and a bookmobile. The library also has a local history and genealogy room and contains government documents dating back to the 19th century. The libraries offer services such as computer classes, book reviews, tax forms, and online book clubs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Libraries_122-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Libraries-122">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Media">\n        Media\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Media">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk\'s daily newspaper is\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Virginian-Pilot" title="The Virginian-Pilot">\n         The Virginian-Pilot\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       . Its alternative papers include the (now defunct)\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Port_Folio_Weekly" title="Port Folio Weekly">\n         Port Folio Weekly\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/New_Journal_and_Guide" title="New Journal and Guide">\n         New Journal and Guide\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , and the online AltDaily.com.\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Inside_Business_(newspaper)" title="Inside Business (newspaper)">\n         Inside Business\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       serves the regional business community with local business news.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_News_Links_123-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_News_Links-123">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Local universities publish their own newspapers:\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_University" title="Old Dominion University">\n        Old Dominion University\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <i>\n        Mace and Crown\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_State_University" title="Norfolk State University">\n        Norfolk State University\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <i>\n        The Spartan Echo\n       </i>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Wesleyan_College" title="Virginia Wesleyan College">\n        Virginia Wesleyan College\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <i>\n        Marlin Chronicles\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_News_Links_123-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_News_Links-123">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Coastal Virginia Magazine\n       </i>\n       is a bi-monthly regional magazine for Norfolk and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads" title="Hampton Roads">\n        Hampton Roads\n       </a>\n       area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_Magazine_124-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_Magazine-124">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Hampton Roads Times\n       </i>\n       is an online magazine for Norfolk and the Hampton Roads area.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is served by a variety of radio stations on the AM and FM dials, with towers located around the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads" title="Hampton Roads">\n        Hampton Roads\n       </a>\n       area. These cater to many different interests, including\n       <a href="/wiki/News" title="News">\n        news\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Talk_radio" title="Talk radio">\n        talk radio\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sports" title="Sports">\n        sports\n       </a>\n       , as well as an eclectic mix of\n       <a href="/wiki/Music" title="Music">\n        musical\n       </a>\n       interests.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_Radio_Links_125-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_Radio_Links-125">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is served by several television stations. The Hampton Roads\n       <a href="/wiki/Media_market" title="Media market">\n        designated market area\n       </a>\n       (DMA) is the 42nd largest in the U.S. with 712,790 homes (0.64% of the total U.S.).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nielsen_126-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nielsen-126">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The major network television affiliates are\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WTKR-TV" title="WTKR-TV">\n        WTKR-TV\n       </a>\n       3 (\n       <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">\n        CBS\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WAVY" title="WAVY">\n        WAVY\n       </a>\n       10 (\n       <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">\n        NBC\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WVEC-TV" title="WVEC-TV">\n        WVEC-TV\n       </a>\n       13 (\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Broadcasting_Company" title="American Broadcasting Company">\n        ABC\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a href="/wiki/WGNT" title="WGNT">\n        WGNT\n       </a>\n       27 (\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_CW_Television_Network" title="The CW Television Network">\n        CW\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WTVZ" title="WTVZ">\n        WTVZ\n       </a>\n       33 (\n       <a href="/wiki/MyNetworkTV" title="MyNetworkTV">\n        MyNetworkTV\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a href="/wiki/WVBT" title="WVBT">\n        WVBT\n       </a>\n       43 (\n       <a href="/wiki/Fox_Broadcasting_Company" title="Fox Broadcasting Company">\n        Fox\n       </a>\n       ), and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WPXV" title="WPXV">\n        WPXV\n       </a>\n       49 (\n       <a href="/wiki/Ion_Television" title="Ion Television">\n        Ion Television\n       </a>\n       ). The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Public_Broadcasting_Service" title="Public Broadcasting Service">\n        Public Broadcasting Service\n       </a>\n       station is\n       <a href="/wiki/WHRO-TV" title="WHRO-TV">\n        WHRO-TV\n       </a>\n       15. Norfolk residents also can receive independent stations, such as\n       <a href="/wiki/WSKY-TV" title="WSKY-TV">\n        WSKY\n       </a>\n       broadcasting on channel 4 from the Outer Banks of North Carolina and\n       <a href="/wiki/WGBS-LD" title="WGBS-LD">\n        WGBS-LD\n       </a>\n       broadcasting on channel 11 from\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton,_Virginia" title="Hampton, Virginia">\n        Hampton\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Several major\n       <a href="/wiki/Film" title="Film">\n        motion pictures\n       </a>\n       have been filmed in and around Norfolk, including\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Rollercoaster_(1977_film)" title="Rollercoaster (1977 film)">\n         Rollercoaster\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       (filmed at the former\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_View_Amusement_Park" title="Ocean View Amusement Park">\n        Ocean View Amusement Park\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Navy_SEALs_(film)" title="Navy SEALs (film)">\n         Navy Seals\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , and\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Mission:_Impossible_III" title="Mission: Impossible III">\n         Mission: Impossible III\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       (partially filmed at the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay_Bridge_Tunnel" title="Chesapeake Bay Bridge Tunnel">\n        Chesapeake Bay Bridge Tunnel\n       </a>\n       ).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IMDB_nor_movies_127-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-IMDB_nor_movies-127">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Central_Radio_controversy">\n        Central Radio controversy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Central Radio controversy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In 2010 the Norfolk Redevelopment and Housing Authority moved to take over the property of Central Radio, a communications and engineering firm, and other businesses and residential properties through eminent domain, and turn the land over to\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_University" title="Old Dominion University">\n        Old Dominion University\n       </a>\n       . In response, Central Radio hung a 375-square foot banner reading, "50 years on this street/78 years in Norfolk/100 workers/Threatened by eminent domain!" The city cited Central Radio for sign code infringement and ordered the banner removed.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2013 the Virginia Supreme Court held that the city\'s attempt to take over the business properties was illegal.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, the U.S. District Court ruled in favor the city regarding the sign removal. In January 2015, the 4th Circuit Court of Appeals affirmed the district court\'s ruling. In April 2015, the Institute for Justice asked the U.S. Supreme Court to hear the case as a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Amendment" title="First Amendment">\n        First Amendment\n       </a>\n       free speech issue.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Infrastructure">\n        Infrastructure\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Infrastructure">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">\n        Transportation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Transportation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main articles:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Transportation_in_Norfolk" title="Transportation in Norfolk">\n        Transportation in Norfolk\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads_Transit" title="Hampton Roads Transit">\n        Hampton Roads Transit\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="375" data-file-width="500" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c8/HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg/200px-HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c8/HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg/300px-HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c8/HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg/400px-HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:HRT_1603_at_Norfolk_General.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hampton Roads Transit bus at\n         <a href="/wiki/Sentara_Norfolk_General_Hospital" title="Sentara Norfolk General Hospital">\n          Sentara Norfolk General Hospital\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="2272" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg/200px-Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg/300px-Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg/400px-Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hampton_Roads_Bridge_Tunnel.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hampton Roads Bridge Tunnel\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3008" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg/200px-PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg/300px-PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg/400px-PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:PortsmouthNorfolkFerry1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Ferry to Portsmouth\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is linked with its neighbors through an extensive network of arterial and\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_Highway_System" title="Interstate Highway System">\n        Interstate highways\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bridge" title="Bridge">\n        bridges\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tunnel" title="Tunnel">\n        tunnels\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bridge-tunnel" title="Bridge-tunnel">\n        bridge-tunnel\n       </a>\n       complexes. The major east-west routes are\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_64_in_Virginia" title="Interstate 64 in Virginia">\n        Interstate 64\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Route_58_(Virginia)" title="U.S. Route 58 (Virginia)">\n        U.S. Route 58\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Boulevard" title="Virginia Beach Boulevard">\n        Virginia Beach Boulevard\n       </a>\n       ) and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Route_60_(Virginia)" title="U.S. Route 60 (Virginia)">\n        U.S. Route 60\n       </a>\n       (Ocean View Avenue). The major north-south routes are\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Route_13_(Virginia)" title="U.S. Route 13 (Virginia)">\n        U.S. Route 13\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Route_460_(Virginia)" title="U.S. Route 460 (Virginia)">\n        U.S. Route 460\n       </a>\n       , also known as\n       <a href="/wiki/Granby_Street" title="Granby Street">\n        Granby Street\n       </a>\n       . Other main roadways in Norfolk include\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_State_Route_403" title="Virginia State Route 403">\n        Newtown Road\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Waterside_Drive" title="Waterside Drive">\n        Waterside Drive\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tidewater_Drive" title="Tidewater Drive">\n        Tidewater Drive\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Military_Highway" title="Military Highway">\n        Military Highway\n       </a>\n       . The Hampton Roads Beltway (I-64,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/I-264_(VA)" title="I-264 (VA)">\n        I-264\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/I-464" title="I-464">\n        I-464\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/I-664" title="I-664">\n        I-664\n       </a>\n       ) makes a loop around Norfolk.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is primarily served by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_International_Airport" title="Norfolk International Airport">\n        Norfolk International Airport\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Air_Transport_Association_airport_code" title="International Air Transport Association airport code">\n        IATA\n       </a>\n       :\n       <b>\n        ORF\n       </b>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Civil_Aviation_Organization_airport_code" title="International Civil Aviation Organization airport code">\n        ICAO\n       </a>\n       :\n       <b>\n        KORF\n       </b>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Aviation_Administration" title="Federal Aviation Administration">\n        FAA\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Location_identifier" title="Location identifier">\n        LID\n       </a>\n       :\n       <b>\n        ORF\n       </b>\n       ), now the region\'s major commercial airport. The airport is located near the Chesapeake Bay, along with the city limits straddling neighboring\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach,_Virginia" title="Virginia Beach, Virginia">\n        Virginia Beach\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ORF_History_130-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ORF_History-130">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Seven airlines provide nonstop services to twenty five destinations. ORF had 3,703,664 passengers take off or land at its facility and 68,778,934 pounds of cargo were processed through its facilities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ORF_Statistics_131-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ORF_Statistics-131">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Newport_News/Williamsburg_International_Airport" title="Newport News/Williamsburg International Airport">\n        Newport News/Williamsburg International Airport\n       </a>\n       also provides commercial air service for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads" title="Hampton Roads">\n        Hampton Roads\n       </a>\n       area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Newport_News.2FWilliamsburg_International_Airport_132-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Newport_News.2FWilliamsburg_International_Airport-132">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       NNWIA is also the only airport in the region with direct international flights, as of February 2013. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Regional_Airport" title="Chesapeake Regional Airport">\n        Chesapeake Regional Airport\n       </a>\n       provides general aviation services and is located five miles (8\xc2\xa0km) outside the city limits.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is served by\n       <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">\n        Amtrak\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Regional" title="Northeast Regional">\n        Northeast Regional\n       </a>\n       service through the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norfolk_(Amtrak_station)" title="Norfolk (Amtrak station)">\n        Norfolk\n       </a>\n       station, located in downtown Norfolk adjacent to\n       <a href="/wiki/Harbor_Park" title="Harbor Park">\n        Harbor Park\n       </a>\n       stadium. The line runs west along\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Southern_Railway" title="Norfolk Southern Railway">\n        Norfolk Southern\n       </a>\n       trackage, paralleling the\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_460_in_Virginia" title="U.S. Route 460 in Virginia">\n        US Route 460\n       </a>\n       corridor to\n       <a href="/wiki/Petersburg,_Virginia" title="Petersburg, Virginia">\n        Petersburg\n       </a>\n       , thence on to\n       <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">\n        Richmond\n       </a>\n       and beyond. A high-speed rail connection at Richmond to both the\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Corridor" title="Northeast Corridor">\n        Northeast Corridor\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Southeast_High_Speed_Rail_Corridor" title="Southeast High Speed Rail Corridor">\n        Southeast High-Speed Rail Corridor\n       </a>\n       are also under study.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SEHSR_133-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SEHSR-133">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Greyhound_Lines" title="Greyhound Lines">\n        Greyhound Lines\n       </a>\n       provides service from a central bus terminal in downtown Norfolk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Today.27s_Bus_134-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Today.27s_Bus-134">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In April 2007, construction of the new $36,000,000 Half Moone Cruise Terminal was completed downtown adjacent to the Nauticus Museum, providing a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State-of-the-art" title="State-of-the-art">\n        state-of-the-art\n       </a>\n       permanent structure for various cruise lines and passengers wishing to embark from Norfolk. Previously, makeshift structures were used to embark/disembark passengers, supplies, and crew.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Half_Moone_Terminal_66-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Half_Moone_Terminal-66">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Intracoastal_Waterway" title="Intracoastal Waterway">\n        Intracoastal Waterway\n       </a>\n       passes through Norfolk. Norfolk also has extensive frontage and port facilities on the navigable portions of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Western_Branch_Elizabeth_River" title="Western Branch Elizabeth River">\n        Western\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Southern_Branch_Elizabeth_River" title="Southern Branch Elizabeth River">\n        Southern\n       </a>\n       Branches of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_River_(Virginia)" title="Elizabeth River (Virginia)">\n        Elizabeth River\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Light_rail" title="Light rail">\n        Light rail\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bus" title="Bus">\n        bus\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ferry" title="Ferry">\n        ferry\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Paratransit" title="Paratransit">\n        paratransit\n       </a>\n       services are provided by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads_Transit" title="Hampton Roads Transit">\n        Hampton Roads Transit\n       </a>\n       (HRT), the regional\n       <a href="/wiki/Public_transport" title="Public transport">\n        public transport\n       </a>\n       system headquartered in Hampton. HRT buses operate throughout Norfolk and South Hampton Roads and onto the Peninsula all the way up to Williamsburg. Other routes travel to\n       <a href="/wiki/Smithfield,_Virginia" title="Smithfield, Virginia">\n        Smithfield\n       </a>\n       . HRT\'s ferry service connects downtown Norfolk to Old Town Portsmouth.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HRT_Service_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HRT_Service-135">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additional services include an HOV express bus to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norfolk_Naval_Base" title="Norfolk Naval Base">\n        Norfolk Naval Base\n       </a>\n       , paratransit services, park-and-ride lots, and the Norfolk Electric Trolley, which provides service in the downtown area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-About_HRT_136-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-About_HRT-136">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Tide_Light_Rail" title="Tide Light Rail">\n        Tide\n       </a>\n       light rail service began operations in August 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HRT_Pressroom_137-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HRT_Pressroom-137">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The light rail is a starter route running along the southern portion of Norfolk, commencing at Newtown Road and passing through stations serving areas such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_State_University" title="Norfolk State University">\n        Norfolk State University\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Harbor_Park" title="Harbor Park">\n        Harbor Park\n       </a>\n       before going through the heart of downtown Norfolk and terminating at\n       <a href="/wiki/Sentara_Norfolk_General_Hospital" title="Sentara Norfolk General Hospital">\n        Sentara Norfolk General Hospital\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Light_Rail_Project_138-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Light_Rail_Project-138">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hampton Roads Transportation, Inc. dispatches Black and White Cabs of Norfolk, Yellow Cab of Norfolk and Norfolk Checker Cab.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Utilities">\n        Utilities\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Utilities">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Water and sewer services are provided by the city\'s Department of Utilities. Norfolk receives its electricity from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dominion_Virginia_Power" title="Dominion Virginia Power">\n        Dominion Virginia Power\n       </a>\n       which has local sources including the Chesapeake Energy Center (a gas power plant), coal-fired plants in\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake,_Virginia" title="Chesapeake, Virginia">\n        Chesapeake\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Southampton_County,_Virginia" title="Southampton County, Virginia">\n        Southampton County\n       </a>\n       , and the Surry Nuclear Power Plant. Norfolk-headquartered\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AGL_Resources#Virginia_Natural_Gas" title="AGL Resources">\n        Virginia Natural Gas\n       </a>\n       , a subsidiary of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AGL_Resources" title="AGL Resources">\n        AGL Resources\n       </a>\n       , distributes\n       <a href="/wiki/Natural_gas" title="Natural gas">\n        natural gas\n       </a>\n       to the city from storage plants in\n       <a href="/wiki/James_City_County,_Virginia" title="James City County, Virginia">\n        James City County\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake,_Virginia" title="Chesapeake, Virginia">\n        Chesapeake\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk\'s water quality has been recognized one of the cleanest water systems in the United States and ranked as the fourth best in the United States by\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Men%27s_Health_(magazine)" title="Men\'s Health (magazine)">\n         Men\'s Health\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Utilities_139-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Utilities-139">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city of Norfolk has a tremendous capacity for clean fresh water. The city owns nine reservoirs: Lake Whitehurst, Little Creek Reservoir, Lake Lawson, Lake Smith, Lake Wright, Lake Burnt Mills, Western Branch Reservoir, Lake Prince and Lake Taylor.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Virginia tidewater area has grown faster than the local freshwater supply. The river water has always been salty, and the fresh groundwater is no longer available in most areas. Currently, water for the cities of Chesapeake and Virginia Beach is pumped from\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Gaston" title="Lake Gaston">\n        Lake Gaston\n       </a>\n       (which straddles the Virginia-North Carolina border) into the City of Norfolk\'s reservoir system and then diverted to the City of Chesapeake for treatment by the City of Chesapeake. Virginia Beach\'s portion of water is treated by the City of Norfolk at Moores Bridges water treatment plant and then piped into Virginia Beach. The pipeline is 76 miles (122\xc2\xa0km) long and 60 inches (1,500\xc2\xa0mm) in diameter. Much of its follows the former\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Right-of-way_(railroad)" title="Right-of-way (railroad)">\n        right-of-way\n       </a>\n       of an abandoned portion of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginian_Railway" title="Virginian Railway">\n        Virginian Railway\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">\n        <a href="#cite_note-141">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is capable of pumping 60 million gallons of water per day; Virginia Beach and Chesapeake are partners in the project.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">\n        <a href="#cite_note-142">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The city provides wastewater services for residents and transports wastewater to the regional Hampton Roads Sanitation District treatment plants.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norfolk_Utilities_139-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norfolk_Utilities-139">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Healthcare">\n        Healthcare\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Healthcare">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:SNGH1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="2272" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/SNGH1.jpg/200px-SNGH1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/SNGH1.jpg/300px-SNGH1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/SNGH1.jpg/400px-SNGH1.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:SNGH1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Sentara Norfolk General Hospital\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Because of the prominence of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Naval_Medical_Center_Portsmouth" title="Naval Medical Center Portsmouth">\n        Naval Medical Center Portsmouth\n       </a>\n       and the Hampton\n       <a href="/wiki/Veterans_Health_Administration" title="Veterans Health Administration">\n        VA\n       </a>\n       Medical Center in Hampton, Norfolk has had a strong role in medicine. Norfolk is served by\n       <a href="/wiki/Sentara_Norfolk_General_Hospital" title="Sentara Norfolk General Hospital">\n        Sentara Norfolk General Hospital\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sentara_Leigh_Hospital" title="Sentara Leigh Hospital">\n        Sentara Leigh Hospital\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Bon_Secours_DePaul_Medical_Center" title="Bon Secours DePaul Medical Center">\n        Bon Secours DePaul Medical Center\n       </a>\n       . The city is also home to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_Hospital_of_The_King%27s_Daughters" title="Children\'s Hospital of The King\'s Daughters">\n        Children\'s Hospital of The King\'s Daughters\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Taylor_Transitional_Care_Hospital" title="Lake Taylor Transitional Care Hospital">\n        Lake Taylor Transitional Care Hospital\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hospital_Listings_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hospital_Listings-143">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Norfolk is home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Virginia_Medical_School" title="Eastern Virginia Medical School">\n        Eastern Virginia Medical School\n       </a>\n       , which is known for its specialists in\n       <a href="/wiki/Diabetes_mellitus" title="Diabetes mellitus">\n        diabetes\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Dermatology" title="Dermatology">\n        dermatology\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Obstetrics" title="Obstetrics">\n        obstetrics\n       </a>\n       . It achieved international fame on March 1, 1980, when Drs. Georgianna and Howard Jones opened the first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/In_vitro_fertilization" title="In vitro fertilization">\n        in vitro fertilization\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">\n        <a href="#cite_note-144">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       clinic in the U.S. at EVMS. The country\'s first in-vitro\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Test-tube_baby" title="Test-tube baby">\n        test-tube baby\n       </a>\n       was born there in December 1981.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jones_Institute_-_About_Us_145-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Jones_Institute_-_About_Us-145">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The international headquarters of\n       <a href="/wiki/Operation_Smile" title="Operation Smile">\n        Operation Smile\n       </a>\n       , a nonprofit organization that specializes in repairing facial deformities in underprivileged children from around the globe, is located in the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Operation_Smile_146-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Operation_Smile-146">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Physicians for Peace,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       a nonprofit that focuses on providing training and education to medical professionals in the developing world, is based in Norfolk.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">\n        Notable people\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norfolk,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Notable people">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">\n       <div class="mw-references-wrap">\n        <ol class="references">\n         <li <span class="reference-text">\n           Mean monthly maxima and minima (i.e. the expected highest and lowest temperature readings at any point during the year or given month) calculated based on data at said location from 1981 to 2010.\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-36">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a December 1945 at the Weather Bureau Office in downtown, and at Norfolk Int\'l since January 1946.
